<UserId.>112370996458327347355< /UserId.><name>Xbox User< /name><date>1517412308807< /date>< Rating>
5< /Rating>
< Review>
Great New find; you can see and taste the quality. A simple menu with complex flavors & food that will keep you coming back! Although our server was great everyone came and checked on us. The bartender was mixing Valentine's Day concoctions and recruited us to participate in a taste test.

The medium-sized room is elegantly decorated. The bathrooms are large and clean. We arrived for an early dinner, the place was mostly empty. By 6:30 every table was full & there were hungry patrons waiting for a seat. Others picked up to-go orders, so people already know about Lotus and Light. I recommend you check it out, and review it for yourself.

Parking is ample & next door to Starbucks. You can enjoy some shopping or hit the grocery market a few doors down. I highly recommend the 50/50 beef and pork rice (it's not on the menu as 50/50). The meat was so tender and flavorful the sauce included was on point.

I had the beef pho my wife had the vegetable tofu. Mine was rich and flavorful I thought hers was a little bland. Overall everything we sampled was fantastic. The service was great. As you can see on receipt, the price is what you would expect. The quality excellent, the space was bright and clean. I give 5 stars with confidence I will be back save me a table!<//Review>

I would recommend this place to anybody who likes Vietnamese food (Thai inspired). We tried the fried tofu, it was super light and super savory (fave). Also recommended would be the Bangkok noodle rolls the pho fillet and the Lotus papaya salad. Just as good as their main entrees and starters are their deserts. Did I mention they have a variety of soju cocktails? Yeah. They do. Try their version of the East Side.<//Review>

<date>1528848398187<//date>< Rate>
5<//Rate>
<text>If you love Golden Deli in San Gabriel you'll love this place more. It's great that I finally don't have to drive all the way to the SGV to get my fix of authentic pho.

What makes this particular pho place stand out from the billion of other pho places in Los Angeles is how darn clean their pho tastes. It doesn't have any MSG, they either use no salt or very little so you can apply your own level of sodium chloride to your liking. The best part of it is the pho broth is SO DANG rich and perfect it doesn't need anything extra. This place has unexpectedly become my new favorite restaurant after a workout. It always makes my body feel like I'm filling it with nutrients and not just a pho equivalent of nightQuil that I need to lay down to digest for several hours after eating.

The same level of rich brothness is the same for their for their veggie pho. The broth is an incredibly rich umami shiitake broth. I've never had a veggie pho that the broth ever stood out like that. It's really really good. They also must steam their veggies over broth because all the steamed veggies were full of the same rich broth flavor. It's as good as their beef pho.

This is also the only pho place that I'll eat tendon in my pho. I appreciate that they cut it up into edible small bite size pieces that are appealing and easy to eat.

Their crunchy wraps and veggie spring roll wraps are also killer. The prices are also very fair for the level of quality you get.

Another small thing that is nice. The noodles in the pho are cooked to order. Have you ever been to a restaurant when you get your pho you have to try to separate all the noodles from being stuck together in a dense ball because they were prepared an hour ago? You won't have that problem here.<//text><Pics>None< /Pics><response>None<//response>< Gmap_id>

If you want cheap prices and SLOW and INEFFICIENT service, this is your company.  Companies should be judged on how they handle problems, not when everything goes the way it should ... why? Because normal is normal and should not be recognized as good.

Problem #1
I ordered 2 sets of office chairs. I was supposed to get $40 off my order per the online promotion. Instead they force applied a coupon for $12 off. I removed the coupon at the checkout and the $40 again got deducted. When I went to pay, they removed the $40 off promo and only gave me the $12 coupon. I only realized it after my order was placed. It seems like they do this on purpose. Show you a $40 off in your cart and then change it at the last minute to give you a lower savings. Ultimately after 2 emails and 3 days, they refunded my money for the difference.

Problem #2

I would rather pay more with a company that is efficient and can handle customer service issues, be accountable for it's actions, and not have trickery in the check out process when offering discounts.

My order number is 101057341. Don't leave a canned answer of how your sorry and work so hard to avoid these issues. Pull up my order and reach out to me. More importantly, send me the merchandise I paid for.< /text>

I recently received this kitchen island from Costway, and it is perfect for my small kitchen. I really needed something that would provide me with not only a nice prep and beverage space, but also some extra storage. This kitchen island boasts two cabinets, one larger and one smaller, as well as two drawers. The shelves in the cabinets are easily adjustable to fit your needs. The cabinets open easy, but are also secure with a magnet closure. The drawers glide open like a dream, but have a stopper, as to not accidentally pull the entire drawer out. If you have kids, like I do, you know how important it is for those drawer stoppers to work. The island also features a knife block on the end. One of my favorite features of this island is that it has wheels to easily move it. This is so convenient for cleaning underneath and behind it. The handle, that is on the end, also helps you easily move the island, but also can be used as a kitchen towel or paper towel rack. Overall, this kitchen island is aesthetically pleasing. The materials used to make this are pretty sturdy. One thing I‚Äôd like to touch on is the directions and packaging. I can‚Äôt tell you how many times I‚Äôve bought things elsewhere where the directions are terrible, and all the hardware is thrown into one bag. That is not the case at all with this! The directions were very clear and easy to follow, and all hardware was bagged separately and labeled. This made putting the island together so much quicker. If you are on the fence about an item, don‚Äôt hesitate! You won‚Äôt be able to find the same quality for the price. Plus, don‚Äôt forget you get fast and free shipping. Do yourself a favor and order; you won‚Äôt be sorry!

I was also in the market for a bunk bed for my kids room. I needed one with solid construction, so it would grow with them but also wanted one that was not going to break the bank. This bunk bed definitely fit the bill. After ordering, it took about 2-3 days to arrive. Everything was well packed and protected. It took my husband about an hour to assemble. The process of putting it together goes so much faster, as they have everything clearly labeled and hardware is sorted out into individual bags. One thing my husband really liked was that the mattress slats were tethered together for each bunk. This takes the guess work out of how many to use or how far to space them. The wood is pretty solid and not the really cheap stuff. The bed is very stable, and I like that it is not squeaky if my kids move, like some other beds. The bottom bunk sits higher off the ground and provides ample room to store stuff under the bed, if you would like. Another plus is that this bed is versatile and can be separated into 2 twin size beds, if we choose to do so. Overall, my kids are absolutely thrilled with their bunk bed, and so am I.</review>

<username>Tim Hobbs< /username><time>1602116571027</time><rating>4</rating>< Review>
The chair comes disassembled and took about 30-45 minutes to put together at a leisurely pace. The instructions could be a bit easier to understand but if you have assembled any furniture it is pretty much the same thing. The hardware comes in a nice little package so you don't have to dig through the box to find parts.

I was impressed by the overall quality. The feel is nice. My daughter thought it was really cool :)

The chair is comfortable and the adjustment options are nice: up/down, arms up/down and swivel in/out, and the recline feature is cool though not sure how practical. To be honest when I tested it out it went so far back I thought I was going to fall backwards. I don't even think I reclined it all the way! The one thing that would be nice is if the arm width could be adjusted - right now it would require adjusting the screws.

I work full time from home so I am pretty decently versed in chair prices and for any decent chair you would pay the same or more, so it seems like a decent price and value. I know that many similar "gamer" chairs can run up to 5x more.</Review>

<gmap_id>0x80dcb5ca7aeb2565:0xa524c555cf6e9b65<//gmap_id><Text>I purchased an office/gaming desk off of Amazon. First thing to note is that this product is claimed to be made by Tangkula, which is actually a company based out of California by the name of Costway. The desk arrived in two separate packages when it could easily been one, which leads me to believe the desktop and support system come from different locations...little odd but whatever.

Both boxes arrive and I start assembly. There are a few surface imperfections in faux wood grain as shown in picture. ‚ÄúWooden‚Äù pieces and the black mid section are adjoined by small wooden pegs and reinforced by metal runners. Seems like the hole thing should more securely fastened together. Hexagonal bolts fasten everything together, but poor quality control made it rough to assemble as receiving holes were not properly reamed out.

Next my issue dealing with customer support arises. I found that my packages did not include 2 of the parts necessary to complete construction. I contacted the actual company Costway through their email found on their website and through here on Amazon. Only way to contact them is through email, and it took a long time to finally get a hold of someone. We spoke via email over the course of several days because they only answer in the middle of the night (EASTERN US TIMEZONE). First they told me they didn‚Äôt have those parts in stock and it would be 25-30 days until they got more in from China. They offered to compensate me $30 for my wait, but I said no and that if the parts were not there within a week I‚Äôd like a refund. So ‚Äúsurprise‚Äù they decided to send me an entire half of the order with all the hardware and legs (could of just taken those missing parts out of the box). Customer service was not rude, but hard to reach and odd to deal with.

After I got my replacement parts I finish putting the desk together as detailed. The remaining bolts holes could also used reamed as I said before. Washers would also help prevent any over torque since they need to be securely tightened to prevent any wobbling. As shown in the picture there is a small 1/8‚Äù gap on one side between faux wood and black mid section due to poor quality control.

Overall the desk looks nice minus the surface imperfections and panel gaps. The adjustable legs are nice since I live in an older home with uneven floors. That does not excuse the missing parts, hard to reach customer service, and poor quality control. I would not make another purchase from Tangkula AKA Costway AKA Any Other Brand They Use.

PROS:
Simple steps for constructions
Looks nice
Adjustable feet

CONS:
Poor quality control
Missing parts upon arrival
Hard to reach manufacturer
Design flaws (should have washers)</Text>< username>

We opened the box, there was no damage to it, everything was in tact and packed perfectly, and then we plugged it in, connected the water supply and turned it on.
As soon as we turned it on the tub started to fill with water. It was able to make ice but the ice fell in the tub of water. I called Costway and was instructed to email their customer service. I couldn't speak to anyone all concerns were to be emailed. I did that and their response times is 24-48hrs. After several emails back and forth sending videos and pics they said the machine was missing the plug and they would send me one. They sent me the plug for the unit 3 different times because i never received it. I finally received it in July, installed the plug, turned the machine on and no leaks! Woo hoo, now I can finally use my ice maker! NOT!!!! Although the machine didn't leak it produced very soft ice and couldn't keep it frozen. All the ice that was made would fall in the tub and melt, until the tub was finally filled with water and half melted ice. It got to the point where the machine would produce ice and it would fall in the tub of water and the water would overflow onto the floor so we had to turn it off. I've been trying to call Costway for the past week. No ring, just busy signal. I also emailed them waiting for a response, which i think is going to come from China which isn't all that great cause they are not very clear with their info. not to mention their instruction manual sucks!  Worst thing ever! The machine also produces a lot of noise to have in a kitchen.
I hate this thing, most of all I hate the customer service offered by Costway. I have a feeling they are going to ask me to get the machine checked or something on my dime, or blame it on me who knows. I'm also going to email Amazon. We are on a budget. I saved up money for this unit. I choose it because it had mostly good reviews. Apparently I got the lemon. All I want is a machine that works. is that too much to ask. Don't buy this unit!!<//text>

<Rating>4<//Rating><review>I purchased a GO PLUS Magnetic Exercise Bike Stationary Belt Drive Indoor Cycling Bike. Upon receiving I noticed there was an incomplete part discovered during assembly. I contacted Costway via email and twitter with picture and information. They responded and sent me the complete molded part. It took some time to recieve the part as that was explained in the initial correspondence and it was close to the time Costway customer service said it would take. While I waited for part I was able to make bike functional in the meantime. But needless to say the bike is solid now with the complete molded part. I give the review 4 stars for that reason. It's winter/snow where I live right now and I have no concern about the elements outside because I have a workout room set up and now this indoor bike to complete my 24 hour fitness area in my place. I'm 56 and I bike often in the summer outside. It's an important part of my complete workouts and have spent more than a few winters suffering by not having that option indoors. I do not have that concern anymore. Anytime day or night it can be GO TIME on this bike. The heavy 30 lb flywheel is just right. The belt drive is whisper quiet. And the magnets. Oh man.... I just rotated the adjustable knob in a full 360¬∞to move the magnets closer to the flywheel. The new resistance level is kickin my butt so my numbers for speed and distance are lower of course on the LCD monitor that also observes time, calorie and heart rate. But that's what great workouts are about. Time to climb that mountain all over again. I can't begin to describe how great the workouts are with this spinner bike. It's full-on intense and worth every minute. Just what I was hoping for when I bought it. I wish the LCD monitor would show miles instead of kilometers but it's not difficult to calculate your kilometers to miles, kph to mph, etc. That would be the other reason I gave 4 stars for this review. In closing. Thanks Costway for a great spinner/indoor bike.
